      <script language="javascript">
       function check_keywords(){
 				//.replace(/ /g,'')
 				var search_keywords = $(".searchbar_1").val();
 				if(search_keywords != "" && (search_keywords.toUpperCase().indexOf("ALERT") >=0 || search_keywords.toUpperCase().indexOf("SCRIPT") >=0)){
 					search_keywords = escape(search_keywords);
 					$(".searchbar_1").val(search_keywords);
 				}
 				return true;
 			}
 
 			function gear_comming_soon(){
 				fb.loadAnchor("gear_commingsoon.html","type:html theme:black width:810px height:492");
 			}
 			function open_video(video_URL){
 				fb.loadAnchor("tmp.php?video_URL="+video_URL,"type:html theme:black width:498px height:333px");
 			}
 			function header_dis_more(aid,obj) {
 				if($("#place_1_"+aid).css("display") == "none") {
 					$("#place_1_"+aid).slideDown("slow");
 					$(obj).addClass("up");					
 				}
 				else {
 					$("#place_1_"+aid).slideUp("slow");
 					$(obj).removeClass("up");
 				}
 			}
 			$(document).ready(function(){
 				$(".product_items").each(function(index,elm){
 					$(this).hover(function() {
 						$($(".pricebox")[index]).addClass('hover');
 						$($(".product_items_text")[index]).addClass('hover');
 						$($(".hovereffect")[index]).css('display','block');
 					},
 					function() {
 						$($(".pricebox")[index]).removeClass('hover');
 						$($(".product_items_text")[index]).removeClass('hover');
 						$($(".hovereffect")[index]).css('display','none');
 					});
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_1').focusin(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == 'WINE SEARCH') {
 						$(this).val('');
 					}
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_1').focusout(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == '') {
 						$(this).val('WINE SEARCH');
 					}
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_2').focusin(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == 'email address') {
 						$(this).val('');
 					}
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_2').focusout(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == '') {
 						$(this).val('email address');
 					}
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_3').focusin(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == 'email address') {
 						$(this).val('');
 					}
 				});
 				$('.searchbar_3').focusout(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).val() == '') {
 						$(this).val('email address');
 					}
 				});		
 				$(".topmenu > span").each(function(index,elm){
 					$(this).hover(function() {
 						var navId = $(this).attr("class").replace("nav","") ;
 						var leftpos = 5;
 						switch(navId) {
 							case '1':
 								leftpos = 5;
 								break;
 							case '2':
 								leftpos = -85;
 								break;
 							case '3':
 								leftpos = -195;
 								break;
 							case '4':
 								leftpos = -315;
 								break;
 							case '5':
 								leftpos = -465;
 								break;
 							case '6':
 								leftpos = -555;
 								break;
 							case '7':
 								leftpos = -645;
 								break;
 						}
 						$("."+$(this).attr("class")+" > div").css("left",leftpos+"px");
 						$("."+$(this).attr("class")+" > div").css("display","block");
 					},
 					function() {
 						$("."+$(this).attr("class")+" > div").css("display","none");
 						$("."+$(this).attr("class")+" > div").css("left","0px");
 					});
 				});
 				var menuYloc = $(".shop").offset().top;
 				$(".shop").click(function() {
 					if($(this).attr("class") == "shop shop_full") {
 						document.location.href = "process_cart.php";
 					}
 				});
 				$(".dropdown_more").click(function() {
 					var aid = $(this).attr("aid");
 					if($("#menu_more_"+aid).css("display") == "none" ) {
 						$("#menu_more_"+aid).slideDown("slow");
 						$(this).children("a").html("View Less");}
 					else {
 						$("#menu_more_"+aid).slideUp("slow");
 						$(this).children("a").html("View More");
 					}
 				});
 				
 				$(".btn_view_details").each(function(index,elm){
 				});
 				
 			});
 			function goto_product_detail_page(pid) {
 				$.ajax({
 					type: "GET",
 					url: "ajaxgetcontent.php",
 					data: "action=product&pid="+pid,
 					success: function(content){
 						tipsWindown("","text:"+content,"950","550","true","","true","");
 						js_scro();
 						$(".tab1").click();
 					}
 				});
 			}
 			function goto_postpone(oid,pid) {
 				fb.loadAnchor("ajaxpostpone.php?oid="+oid+"&pid="+pid, "type:html theme:black width:420px height:342");
 			}
 			function js_scro() {
 				var item = $("#tab3");
 				$(".overview").each(function(index,elm){
 					var tabid = $(this).attr('id');
 					$("."+tabid).bind({
 						click:function(){
 							var item = $("#"+tabid);
 							item.jscroll({
 								W:"8px"
 								,BgUrl:""
 								,Bg:"#cccccc"
 								,Bar:{
 										Pos:"up"
 										,Bd:{Out:"#A01F62",Hover:"#A01F62"}
 										,Bg:{Out:"#A01F62",Hover:"#A01F62",Focus:"#A01F62"}
 									}
 								,Btn:{
 									btn:false
 									,uBg:{Out:"black",Hover:"#ffffff",Focus:"orange"}
 									,dBg:{Out:"black",Hover:"#ffffff",Focus:"orange"}
 								}
 								,Fn:function(){}
 							});					
 						}
 					});
 				});
 			}
 			function bestadd_to_cart(combo_id,products_id,qty){
 				if($("#listquanity_"+products_id).length > 0 && parseInt($("#listquanity_"+products_id).attr("lmqty")) > parseInt($("#listquanity_"+products_id).val()) ){
 					alert("This wine must be ordered in a minimum quantity of "+$("#listquanity_"+products_id).attr("lmqty")+" bottles");
 					return false;
 				}
 				if($("#listquanity_"+products_id).val() != "" && parseInt($("#listquanity_"+products_id).val()) > 0) {
 					qty = $("#listquanity_"+products_id).val();
 				}
 				if($("#id_product_qty").length > 0 && parseInt($("#id_product_qty").attr("lmqty")) > parseInt($("#id_product_qty").val()) ){
 					alert("This wine must be ordered in a minimum quantity of "+$("#id_product_qty").attr("lmqty")+" bottles");
 					return false;
 				}
 				if($("#id_product_qty").val() != "" && parseInt($("#id_product_qty").val()) > 0) {
 					qty = $("#id_product_qty").val();
 				}
 				g_js.windows.mask.busy.show();
 				$.ajax({
 					url: "ajaxcartoption.php",
 					data: "action=add_item&combo_id="+combo_id+"&products_id="+products_id+"&qty="+qty+"&wish_id=0",
 					success: function(v){
 						if(v < 0){
 							$.ajax({
 								type: "GET",
 								url: "ajaxget.php",
 								data: "action=check_stock&pid="+products_id+"&ire_add=1",
 								success: function(rqty){
 									g_js.windows.mask.busy.close();
 									alert("Sorry, we only have \"X\" wines available.".replace('"X"',rqty));
 								}
 							});
 						}
 						else {
 							$(".shop").addClass("shop_full");
 							if($("#id_create_popup").length > 0){
 								g_js.windows.html.close_popup();
 							}
 							if($("#windownbg").length > 0){
 								$("#windownbg").remove();
 								$("#windown-box").fadeOut("slow",function(){
 									$(this).remove();
 								});
 							}
 							setTimeout(function(){
 								g_js.windows.mask.busy.close();
 								alert("Your item has been added to your shopping cart!");
 								$("html,body").animate({scrollTop:0},120);
 							},1500);			
 						}
 					}
 				});
 			}
 			function bestadd_to_cart2(){
 				var combo_id = 0;
 				var qty = $("#id_product_qty").val();
 				var product_type = $("#id_n_product_type").html();
 				var products_id = $("#id_n_parent_product_id").html();
 				bestadd_to_cart(combo_id,products_id,qty);
 			}
 			function best_delete_item(pid){
 				$.ajax({
 					url: "ajaxcartoption.php",
 					data: "action=delete_item&pid="+pid,
 					success: function(v){
 						window.location.href = window.location.href;
 					}
 				});
 			}

         <script>
          var current_x;
 			function auto_play(){
 				//
 				var size_a=$(".royalControlNavCenterer a").size();
 				//
 				auto_p=setInterval("click_current("+size_a+")",6000);
 				$("#auto_play_a").css('display','none');
 				$("#stop_play_a").css('display','block');
 			}
 			function click_current(size){
 				//
 				var current_a=$(".royalControlNavCenterer a.current").attr('id');
 				current_x=current_a.replace('s','');
 				current_x++;
 				if(current_x>size) current_x=1;
 				$("#s"+current_x).click();
 			}
 			function stop_play(){
 				clearInterval(auto_p);
 				$("#auto_play_a").css('display','block');
 				$("#stop_play_a").css('display','none');
 			}
 			jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

 					slideSpacing:0
 				});
 				auto_play();
 				$('.arrow.right, .arrow.left ').hide();
 			});

       <script language="javascript">
        function dis_more(aid,obj) {
 				if($("#more"+aid).css("display") == "none") {
 					$("#more"+aid).slideDown("slow");
 					$(obj).addClass("up");					
 				}
 				else {
 					$("#more"+aid).slideUp("slow");
 					$(obj).removeClass("up");
 				}
 			}
 			$(document).ready(function(){
 				$(".btn_clear").click(function() {
 					if($(this).attr("id") == "clearprices") {
 						$(".by_price_line").each(function(idx,obj){
 							if($(obj).attr("sel") == "1" ) {
 								js_category.generate_search_filter(this);
 								$(obj).attr("sel","0");
 								$(obj).css("background-position","0px 0px");
 							}
 						});
 					}
 					else {
 						$(".left_box_text." + $(this).attr("id").replace("clear","") + " > div").each(function(index,elm){
 							if($(this).attr("sel") == "1") {
 								js_category.generate_search_filter(this);
 								$(this).attr("sel","0").css("background-position","0px 0px");
 							}
 						});
 					}
 					$(".more"+$(this).attr("id").replace("clear","") + " > div").each(function(index,elm){
 						if($(this).attr("sel") == "1") {
 							js_category.generate_search_filter(this);
 							$(this).attr("sel","0").css("background-position","0px 0px");
 						}
 					});
 				});
 				$(".more").click(function() {
 					if($(".more"+$(this).attr("id").replace("more","")).css("display") == "none") {
 						$(".more"+$(this).attr("id").replace("more","")).slideDown("slow");
 						$(this).removeClass("more");
 						$(this).addClass("less");
 					}
 					else {
 						$(".more"+$(this).attr("id").replace("more","")).slideUp("slow");
 						$(this).removeClass("less");
 						$(this).addClass("more");
 					}
 				});
 			});
       </script>

        <script language="javascript">
         $(document).ready(function(){
 				$("#arrow_left_feature").click(function(){
 					if($("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi") == "1"){
 						return false;
 					}
 					$("#center-featureproducts:not(:animated)").animate({marginLeft:'+=732'},"slow",function(){
 						set_iccp(parseInt($("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi"))-1);
 						$("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi",parseInt($("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi")) - 1);
 					});
 				});
 				$("#arrow_right_feature").click(function(){
 					var rvi_content = parseInt($("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi"));
 					var rvc_content = parseInt($("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvc"));
 					if(rvi_content == rvc_content){
 						return false;
 					}
 					$("#center-featureproducts:not(:animated)").animate({marginLeft:'-=732'},"slow",function(){
 						$("#center-featureproducts").attr("rvi",rvi_content+1);
 						set_iccp(rvi_content+1);
 					});
 				});
 			});
 			function set_iccp(icp){
 				$(".icp").each(function(index,elm){
 					if($(this).attr("id") == "iccp"+icp){
 						$(this).attr("src","jsbanner/home_slide_btn1.png");
 					}
 					else{
 						$(this).attr("src","jsbanner/home_slide_btn2.png");
 					}
 				});
 			}
        </script>

                   The 2013 Las Gravas, a blend that has been changing through the years and that in 2013 was 70% Monastrell with 15% each Garnacha and Syrah, had an extended levage and was only bottled in July 2015, so it's been released later than the other wines from that vintage. This traditional red from north-facing vineyards on sandy soils covered with big boulders fermented with indigenous yeasts and matured in barrel for some 19 months. If last time I thought the 2012 could have been the best Las Gravas ever, this time I have the same feeling with this 2013 from a cooler vintage which allowed for a slower ripening of the grapes and better acidity and freshness in the wine. The wine might be slightly marked by the levage and still has some spicy aromas nicely interwoven with notes of bright red cherries, raspberries and flowers, with the signature thyme and rosemary...Of course it can be drunk now, especially with food, but I'd wait to pull the cork, as this should be a fantastic bottle of Las Gravas in a few years. - Luis Gutierrez- Wine Advocate #225

                <div class="hovereffect" style="display: none;">
                 <div class="rating_container">
                 </div>
                 <div class="product_shortdesc_l">
                  <div>
                   <div>
                    We go back a long way with this domaine, and their 2017 is arguably one of te best buys on pink wine values we have seen this year. Located in the Costieres des Nimes at the southern end of the Rhone Valley. This vineyard is covered with the round rocks that you see in Chateauneuf to the north (hence the reference to galets) which add a subtle mineral character to the rose. The main show is red berry flanked by notes yellow atone fruit and a touch of both white pepper and garrigue.
                   </div>
                   <div>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    The style here is definitely old school, with a rather broad fruit component but just the right touch of acidity to keep it fresh on the palate. The mix here is a pretty standard one of 50% Syrah, 40% Grenache, and 10% Mourvdre, but they produce a lot of red win so the juice comes mainly from saignee. The wine has a bit more size than some pinks which allows it to play with a wider array of grilled fare, and the price definitely makes it easier to swallow.
                   </div>
                  </div>

        <script language="javascript">
         $(document).ready(function(){
 				$("#arrow_left_new").click(function(){
 					if($("#center-newproducts").attr("rvi") == "1"){
 						return false;
 					}
 					$("#center-newproducts:not(:animated)").animate({marginLeft:'+=732'},"slow",function(){
 						$("#center-newproducts").attr("rvi",parseInt($("#center-newproducts").attr("rvi")) - 1);
 					});
 				});
 				$("#arrow_right_new").click(function(){
 					var rvi_content = parseInt($("#center-newproducts").attr("rvi"));
 					var rvc_content = parseInt($("#center-newproducts").attr("rvc"));
 					if(rvi_content == rvc_content){
 						return false;
 					}
 					$("#center-newproducts:not(:animated)").animate({marginLeft:'-=732'},"slow",function(){
 						$("#center-newproducts").attr("rvi",rvi_content+1);
 					});
 				});
 			});
        </script>

   <script language="javascript">
    function chechk_sub_email() {
 					if(js_validate_mail($("#sub_email").val())){
 						$.ajax({
 							type: "GET",
 							url: "ajax_sub_email.php",
 							data: "action=sub_email&email="+$("#sub_email").val(),
 							success: function(content){
 								if(content == true) {
 									alert("Congratulations! You have successfully subscribed to our newsletter!");
 								}
 								else {
 									alert(content);
 								}
 							}
 						});
 						return false;
 					}
 					else {
 						return false;
 					}
 				}
 				function chechk_sub_email2() {
 					if(js_validate_mail($("#sub_email2").val())){
 						$.ajax({
 							type: "GET",
 							url: "ajax_sub_email.php",
 							data: "action=sub_email&email="+$("#sub_email2").val(),
 							success: function(content){
 								if(content == true) {
 									alert("Congratulations! You have successfully subscribed to our newsletter!");
 								}
 								else {
 									alert(content);
 								}
 							}
 						});
 						return false;
 					}
 					else {
 						return false;
 					}
 				}
 				$(document).ready(function(){ 
 				$(".tabright > a > div").each(function(index,elm){
 					var obj_class = $(this).attr("class").replace("_link","_box");
 					$(this).hover(function() {
 						$(this).attr("mindex",$(this).css("z-index"));
 						$(this).css("z-index","7777777");
 						var obj_wdith = 50- $("."+obj_class).css("width").replace("px","");
 						obj_wdith += "px";
 						$("."+obj_class).stop().animate({left:""+obj_wdith},1000);
 						$("."+obj_class).css("z-index","8888888");
 					},
 					function() {
 						$("."+obj_class).stop().animate({left:"480px"},2000);
 						$(this).css("z-index",$(this).attr("mindex"));
 					});
 				});
 				$(".tab_yt_link").each(function(index,elm){
 					var obj_class = $(this).attr("class").replace("_link","_box");
 					$(this).hover(function() {
 						$(this).attr("mindex",$(this).css("z-index"));
 						$(this).css("z-index","7777777");
 						var obj_wdith = 50- $("."+obj_class).css("width").replace("px","");
 						obj_wdith += "px";
 						$("."+obj_class).stop().animate({left:""+obj_wdith},1000);
 						$("."+obj_class).css("z-index","8888888");
 					},
 					function() {
 						$("."+obj_class).stop().animate({left:"480px"},2000);
 						$(this).css("z-index",$(this).attr("mindex"));
 					});
 				});
 
 			
 				var minheight = $(window).height() - 450;
 				if(minheight < 450) {
 					minheight = 450;
 				}
 				$(".centerbanner").css("min-height",minheight);
 			});
   </script>
